2 
 
二、 英文摘要及關鍵詞 
Due to forthcoming large scale deployment of RFID systems, many RFID related 
issues have gained significant attention. One of the emerge considerations is the reader 
collision (or interference) problem when a large number of readers are utilized in a limited 
space. The recent EPCglobal UHF Class-1 Generation-2 standard defines a “Dense Reader 
Mode” to avoid this problem. However, the endorsed solution succeeds only under an 
assumption that the coverage of each reader is mutually exclusive (without overlapped 
region). In order to satisfy the condition, a low level reader protocol that can fully control 
each reader’s RF parameters to limit its coverage is ratified in the EPCglobal architecture 
framework. Consequently, it is necessary to seamlessly incorporate both technologies in the 
physical layer and the medium access control layer to conduct a high performance passive 
UHF RFID system in dense reader environment. 
In this proposal, a study on automatic deployment of passive UHF RFID system in a 
dense reader environment is proposed. Not only do we consider novel designs in the 
physical layer and in the medium access control layer individually, but also use cross-layer 
optimization technique to improve the overall system performance. In the physical layer, we 
proposed a novel smart antenna reader design. Taking advantages of the smart antenna 
technology, a smart antenna reader will be able to dynamically change its coverage using 
the adaptive beam-forming technique to prevent uncovered area (where tags cannot be read) 
and overlapped area (where reader interference occurs), and can achieve higher tag read rate 
using spatial division multiple access scheme. Furthermore, a smart antenna reader can 
more precisely estimate its location using an innovative hybrid RFID and smart antenna 
localization technique. 
On the other hand, we will develop a corresponding low level reader protocol in the 
medium access control layer to control all smart antenna readers in the region. Hence, a 
proposed system administrative center can collect information of coverage and location 
from each reader through a customized low level reader protocol, and then can coordinate 
the behavior of each individual reader in the controlled region according to the collected 
information. 
The ultimate objective of this three year proposal is to create a self-adaptive RFID 
system that can automatically adjust its configuration, regardless changes of system 
deployment, to achieve optimal performance in terms of maximal throughput (tag read rate) 
and minimal uncovered area. According to the research trend in RFID system (particularly 
in the physical layer), an RFID system research with merely simulation results but 
experimental validations is usually considered insufficient. Thus, this project not only will 
verify the proposed theories via simulations but also will carry on practical implementations 
based on software defined radio technology to confirm our theoretical results. 
This report presents the first year research outcome of this project. 
Keywords: RFID, Smart Antenna, Anti-collision, Dense reader mode, Software Defined 
Radio, CDMA, SDMA, cross layer, localization, self-adaptation.  
4 
 
標籤衝突問題，已有了相當多的研究[11-24]。一般而言，於射頻辨識系統中，阿羅哈
類演算法效率優於樹狀結構類演算法[11, 12, 16]。以 Gen2標準為例[4]，規範訂定的
正是一種動態訊框時槽阿羅哈（adaptive framed slotted ALOHA）演算法，稱之為 Q
演算法（Q-algorithm）。於[14]中，申請人利用連續衝突或閒置時槽偵測（burst 
collision/idle slot detection）估測標籤數目，對此演算法提出效能改進辦法。該
演算法效能，仰賴於正確標籤數目估測，因此當環境中標籤過多時常造成讀取效能下
降。由於阿羅哈類演算法無法完全防止標籤衝突發生，因此可能產生標籤經過長期詢問
（Query）之後，仍然無法辨識的問題。雖然該問題可以動態訊框大小調整來解決[25, 
26]，但阿羅哈演算法畢竟為一種低效能的多重接取（multiple access）方法[27]。綜
觀現有之標籤防衝突演算法，多為 TDMA 方式，使得其性能受到侷限。因此，若要大幅
提升其系統效能，勢必要如同其他先進通訊系統，結合其他多重接取方法。 
除了上述分時多工技術之外， [28-32]研究中分別提出以分碼多重接取（Code 
Division Multiple Access, CDMA）技術，結合分時多重接取技術以提升標籤之讀取效
能；[31]使用 CDMA 技術來解決碰撞問題，但此技術要實現在射頻辨識系統上之複雜度
甚高且需改變現有標籤架構及現行標準。而在分頻多重接取（Frequency Division 
Multiple Access, FDMA）系統上，[33-35]則使用多載波(multi-carrier)技術來降低
標籤衝突發生。申請人對上述方法，都曾提出論文探討，但其複雜度過高且對系統效能
增進有限，為上述技術所遭遇之瓶頸。 
前述演算法，多未考慮讀取器、標籤之擺設空間、位置、讀取器與標籤相對角度等
因素，[36]首先提出在射頻辨識系統上結合分區多重接取與分時多重接取技術，此篇論
文在硬體中加入相位轉移器，使波束可以依照標籤所在之位置改變角度，增加了波束涵
蓋範圍；此方法必須依靠硬體控制，並無法主動適應標籤之位置改變，只能被動的使用
切換方式更改波束。[37, 38]結合了波束切換(switch beam)及波束掃描(beam scanning)
技術，使讀取器與標籤之間傳輸死角大為減少。最近研究於[39, 40]中，提出分時多重
接取技術加入波束構成技術，將接收到之訊號與不同權重向量運算以改變波束方向，此
方法能適應性調整波束中涵蓋標籤數量，並依環境隨時改變波束大小及方向，有效降低
標籤衝突機率。但目前該研究僅限於單一讀取器，尚未考慮於多讀取器環境之相互干擾。 
二、 射頻辨識系統及智慧型天線定位相關研究 
隨著普及計算、資產追蹤、殘障人士及自動導航輔助的需求擴大，近來定位系統研
究已獲得了相當的重視。射頻辨識系統具有非接觸式通訊、高傳輸資料率及安全性、不
須直接路徑傳導(Non-Line-of-Sight, NLOS)、體積小以及成本較低等優點，因此適用
於室內定位運用，近年來已有許多論文探討此技術之應用[41]。超高頻射頻辨識系統應
用於室內定位可區分為兩大類：讀取器定位以及標籤定位。在讀取器定位應用上，如讀
取器被安裝於行動裝置上，藉由讀取環境中已知位置的主動式或被動式參考標籤
(reference tag)，可估測讀取器及其所在行動裝置位置，也可追蹤其位移資訊及動向。
目前已有甚多讀取器室內定位及相關演算法研究[42-59]。於[43]中，將被動式參考標
籤置於地板或是天花板上，並以四方型排列，行動讀取器經由讀取標籤相對位置，利用
權重平均(weighted average method)演算法估算其位置，但其缺點在於須使用大量之
6 
 
定位，則是利用主動式標籤發射信號到讀取器，由指向性天線或陣列天線求得抵達讀取
器之訊號入射角度，再由所得之直射路徑(Line-of-Sight)的角度去測量出此標籤的方
向。因此近年來結合兩種或更多種定位技術之定位演算法已經被提出[79, 80]，像是結
合抵達時間/ 角度定位法(Hybrid TOA/AOA Positioning, HTAP)是結合到達時間定位和
到達角度定位來估算標籤的位置，此定位法主要的優點在於藉由多種的定位參數來提供
更精確的標籤估測、更值得信賴的综合定位參數。近年已有文獻使用智慧型天線技術於
讀取器定位[58]以及標籤定位[66]，[58]中讀取器利用陣列天線訊號處理演算法，估測
參考標籤與讀取器之間之角度以及距離，計算出讀取器位置。[66] 使用軟體無線電 USRP
開發之雙天線讀取器，利用各天線接收之標籤訊號相位差，求得標籤之位置。唯其應用
為定位 433MHz 主動標籤，其讀取器較類似一般通訊系統之收發機，與本案之讀取器完
全不同。本計劃開發應用於被動是射頻辨識系統之高性能智慧型天線讀取器，將結合智
慧型天線技術與 RFID 定位方法，以具有讀取器室內定位之能力，並以資完成系統自動
佈建最佳化之目標。 
三、 密集讀取器模式射頻辨識系統相關研究 
在被動式射頻辨識系統實際應用時，勢必有多部讀取器同時在同一環境中使用。因
此在[4]中特別將密集讀取器模式(dense reader mode)列入規範。當多部讀取器同時運
行時會造成讀取器與讀取器干擾(reader-to-reader interference)問題，簡稱為讀取
器碰撞問題(reader collision)。目前探討密集讀取器環境問題之文獻有[15, 81-92]。
而在[81, 85, 93] 中，所探討之讀取器與標籤干擾問題，已於[4]中，因標籤規範改進、
及密集讀取器模式制定而受到改善。[82, 84, 91] 則在探討如何在密集讀取器模式最
佳化讀取器設置(deployment)及讀取器同步問題。然而於密集讀取器模式中，仍存在不
同讀取器於相同覆蓋範圍，同時傳送讀取器指令，造成標籤無法識別讀取器指令之讀取
器干擾問題。為了使讀取器碰撞對於 RFID 系統的影響更容易被評估，[94]提出
interrogation-range-reduction rate (IRRR)分析方法，此方法使讀取器碰撞率在變
動環境中能更有效率地被分析。解決讀取器碰撞之方法，於文獻[83]中採用歐洲規範
ETSI，基於載波感測多重接取技術之先聽後說(Listen Before Talk)[92]，此方法基於
分頻多重接取概念下，讀取器監視通道是否被使用，當通道為閒置狀態時才得以使用，
避免同通道干擾，但先聽後說(LBT)缺乏通道使用規劃，降低頻譜使用效率，且當兩部
以上讀取器同時監視同一通道，必定造成碰撞問題，因此[87]提出適應性跳頻(Adaptive 
Channel Hopping, ACH)演算法，基於先聽後說(LBT)原則之下，當兩部以上讀取器偵測
閒置(idle)通道，使用隨機後退(Random Back-off)方式，降低其碰撞機率。近期一個
密集環境有效讀取器碰撞避免演算法在[95]中被提出，此方法先將讀取器隨機分組並按
順序對標籤讀取，能有效避免讀取器碰撞。為瞭解決碰撞且維持系統讀取率，[89]中提
出適應性功率控制(adaptive power control)方法，讀取器將參數傳送至媒體存取控制
層(MAC)以完成動態調整功率，減少讀取器間的重疊覆蓋範圍，來解決讀取器之間的干
擾。除了上述演算法，[96-98]分別使用基因演算法等計算，將基於分區多重接取與最
佳通道選擇等相關演算法解決讀取器碰撞問題。其中[98]提出之使用智慧型天線方法與
本案構想相似；但該文獻僅提出簡化模擬結果，無法探知其應用成效。 
8 
 
應性調整智慧型天線讀取器參數。在密集讀取器環境中使用智慧型天線讀取器以波束合
成方法避免與其他讀取器覆蓋區域重疊，以充分覆蓋所有區域，來解決標籤衝突及降低
讀取器互相干擾機率。並透過實作智慧型天線讀取器及其相關通訊協定，以實際瞭解
RFID系統之關鍵問題，並可用以驗證研究所提出理論成果。 
 
四、 研究方法： 
 
  本計劃預定為三年期之研究計畫，計劃重心放在讀取器發展以及系統設計；計劃的目
標為建立一個使用超高頻智慧型天線讀取器之高效能密集式射頻辨識系統。在這三年計劃
中，第一年我們將分析智慧型天線讀取器效能與應用其於密集式讀取器環境模擬；同時，
利用軟體無線電開發具有陣列天線讀取器。在第二年，我們將延續第一年開發之模擬系
統，以智慧型天線讀取器，進行結合 RFID 與智慧型天線定位技術研究；同時開發與第一
年發展之智慧型天線讀取器對應之低階讀取器協定（LLRP）。在第三年，我們將結合第一
年與第二年之研究，利用智慧型天線讀取器之覆蓋區域（coverage）及其位置估測資訊，
研究能自我調適（self-adaptive）之被動式超高頻密集式射頻辨識系統；同時實際開發
所需之中樞控制系統，透過第二年所開發之特定低階讀取器協定，實際控制多部智慧型天
線讀取器，以驗證我們所提之理論。 
  此報告為第一年研究成果。 
 
五、 結果與討論 
 
第一年計劃中規畫了三項主要工作：智慧型天線讀取器效能研究、LLRP 模擬、以軟
體無線電實作智慧型天線讀取器。其中對智慧型天線讀取器效能研究部分，我們採行軟體
模擬驗證，與預期結果及其他文獻結果相符。於 LLRP模擬部分，已完成 RFID建置環境模
擬，目前正研究與智慧型天線讀取器連結至相關協定。以軟體無線電實作智慧型天線讀取
器亦有若干進展；結合本計畫及主持人所參與其他相關計畫，我們已能以軟體無線電平台
結合陣列天線實際進行訊號來向估測，其獲取訊號來向參數可為後續計畫研究使用。 
 
六、 成果自評： 
   
 本計畫已按照計畫書規劃進度完成了原訂之三項目標，並分別於理論突破及具體實現
兩方面獲得如預期之成果。參與之學生藉由實際之讀取器開發對 RFID 系統獲得深刻了
解，相信藉由本計畫之研究可對國內之 RFID 相關研究及產業能有所貢獻。本計畫所進行
相關研究成果，已發表 SCI國際期刊二篇及國際會議論文二篇。而第一年度之進度如期完
成，也對本計畫之後續延伸研究奠定了良好的基礎。

2Chair’s Welcome
The Steering Committee for 
2011 IEEE International Sym-
posium on Antennas and 
Propagation and USNC/URSI 
National Radio Science Meet-
ing welcomes you to Spokane, 
Washington for what we be-
lieve will be both a productive 
and pleasurable event. The 
technical program will cover 
a vast array of electromag-
netic topics, including the latest 
breakthroughs in antenna design, wireless communications, 
exotic materials, biomedical applications and numerical meth-
ods, to name just a few. The technical program will be aug-
mented by a series of short courses that are designed to teach 
and inform attendees about the latest advances in electromag-
netic science, engineering, and applications. 
The conference hotel that we have selected is truly a one-of-
the-kind historic hotel of the utmost elegance. Constructed 
in 1914 and renovated in 1998 using $44M in funds, the 
Davenport Hotel retains all its original charm while providing 
all the modern amenities of a five star rated hotel. The techni-
cal program will be held in the Spokane Convention Center 
(SCC), which is about six city blocks (a pleasant 15 minute 
walk) away from the Hotel and Tower. (Free transportation 
between sites will be made available morning through night 
for those who wish to avoid walking.) The Center has also 
undergone a recent renovation, making it an aesthetically com-
fortable and modern meeting space. It is located next to the 
pristine Spokane River and the 100 acre Riverfront Park, within 
walking distance to fine shopping, theaters (including a 3D 
IMAX) and restaurants of various ethnic varieties and styles.
We will open the conference on Sunday, July 3rd with a re-
ception at the Davenport Hotel. On Monday, July 4th, we will 
host a free salmon barbeque next to the Spokane River on the 
grounds of the Convention Center. Given that this a national 
holiday for the United States, we will have a unique view of 
the July 4th fireworks that will be launched on the other side 
of the river. 
We look forward to visiting with you in what we think will be 
a unique event that is both professionally and personally re-
warding.
Jeffrey L. Young
Steering Committee, Chair

12
Short Courses
sunday, July 3, 08:00 - 17:00
SC1	 Dielectric	Resonator	Antennas,	Theory,	Design	
and	Applications	with	Recent	Advancement
Speaker: Ahmed A. Kishk, University of Mississippi, USA
Location: SCC-201A
An overview for the development of the dielectric resonator 
antennas will be provided. Theory of operation will be discussed 
to provide basic understanding. Excitation mechanisms such as 
probe, slot, image line and waveguides are presented. Mutual 
coupling and wide scanning capabilities are considered. 
Techniques for broadband and size reduction of the DRA are 
presented. Recent developments of DR as a multifunction device 
for antennas and microwave circuits as a low and high Q-factor 
simultaneously will be provided.
SC2	 Reflector	Antenna	Design	and	Analysis
Speaker: Peter Meincke, TICRA, Denmark
Location: SCC-201B
The course gives an introduction to the design and analysis of 
single and dual reflector antennas, center-fed as well as offset. 
After a review of the analysis methods commonly employed for 
space- and Earth-station reflector antennas, the basic design 
principles are presented. First, single and dual spot-beam 
antennas are considered with the relation between size, feed 
illumination, directivity, and sidelobe level. Second, the influence 
of blockage by struts, subreflector, and feed is discussed. Third, 
the origin of cross polarization in offset designs is addressed 
and it is shown how to improve the polarization characteristics in 
dual reflector systems by employing the Mizuguchi compensation 
principle. Hands-on experience in reflector antenna design 
is obtained during the course by using the software package 
GRASP (participants must bring their own laptop).
SC3	 Electromagnetic	Band	Gap	(EBG)	Structures	in	
Antenna	Engineering:	From	Fundamentals	to	
Recent	Advances
Speaker: Yahya Rahmat-Samii, University of California, 
Los Angeles, USA, and Fan Yang, University of 
Mississippi, USA
Location: SCC-201C
This comprehensive and application-oriented short course on the 
state-of-the-art in electromagnetic band gap (EBG) engineering 
explains the theories, designs, and antenna applications of 
EBG structures. The course will start with an overview of the 
EBG research history and important discoveries. An accurate 
and efficient FDTD/PBC algorithm will be presented for general 
periodic structures analysis. Next, detailed presentations will be 
provided on the unique electromagnetic features and diverse 
functional designs of EBG structures. Furthermore, a wealth of 
practical antenna examples with design details and measurement 
14
sunday, July 3, 13:00 - 17:00
SC7	 Transient	Analysis	of	Electromagnetic	Waves	
Based	on	Numerical	Inversion	of	Laplace	
Transform
Speaker: Qingsheng Zeng, Communications Research Centre 
Canada
Location: SCC-202A
This short course addresses one method based on numerical 
inversion of Laplace transform (NILT), which overcomes the 
restrictions in previous approaches, leads to good accuracy 
in both late and early time, and has a simple algorithm, short 
calculation time, small required memory size and readily 
controlled error. To our knowledge, this would be the first time 
that systematically treats the theory of NILT and its application in 
the transient analysis of electromagnetic waves. This short course 
highlights how to overcome the restrictions of NILT, and places the 
emphasis on how to extend and apply this method to a variety 
of cases.
SC8	 Antenna	Design	for	Mobile	Terminals
Speaker: Zhijun Zhang, Tsinghua University, China
Location: SCC-202B
The lecturer is an antenna engineer turned professor who has 
worked at Apple, Nokia and Amphenol. This is a comprehensive 
course for fresh and intermediate engineers involved in antenna 
design. The course instructs attendees through all aspects of real 
world antenna designs, which includes how to make an stable 
antenna fixture, designing various types of antennas, designing 
an antenna with good manufacturability, using various matching 
technique to improve antenna performance, setting up production 
measurement for mass manufacturing, and making antenna SAR 
and HAC Compliant. Most popular antenna categories, such as 
internal PIFA, integral IFA, internal folded monopole, ceramic 
antennas, stubby antennas and whip stubby antennas, are 
introduced in the course. The course focuses on the basic principle 
of each kind of antenna and emphasizes on key parameters of 
antenna optimization. Complimentary matching software, which 
accompanies with the course, is provided so readers can practice 
various antenna matching technique and design matching circuits 
for real projects.
Friday, July 8, 08:00 - 17:00
SC9	 CEM	Algorithms	for	EMC/EMI	Modeling:	
Electrically	Large	(Antennas	on	Platform)	and	
Small	(SI	in	ICs	and	Packaging)	Problems
Speaker: Jin-Fa Lee and Peng Zhen, Ohio State University, 
USA
Location: SCC-201A
In this lecture, we present our on-going efforts in combating the 
multi-scale electromagnetic problems, both electrically large 
(antennas on platform) and electrically small but complex (SI in 
ICs) through the use of nonconventional PDE methods that are 
non-conformal. The non-conformal numerical methods relax the 
16
acceleration techniques for the finite-difference time-domain 
(FDTD) method, the frequency-domain method of moments 
(MoM), and finite element method (FEM). In addition, we will 
discuss acceleration of other algorithms useful in CEM and signal 
processing such as FFTs. The attendee will walk away from the 
course with an understanding of practical GPU concepts and 
software examples of accelerated CEM applications.
Friday, July 8, 08:00 - 12:00
SC13	 Calderon	Preconditioning	in	Computational	
Electromagnetics
Speaker: Francesco Andriulli, TELECOM Bretagne, France, 
and Eric Michielssen, University of Michigan, USA
Location: SCC-202B
This course will provide an introduction to Calderon preconditioning 
techniques for integral equations pertinent to the analysis of 
electromagnetic boundary value problems. Calderon methods 
permit the construction of rapidly convergent iterative solvers for 
electric and combined field integral equations and as such are 
a perfect complement to fast multipole and related accelerators. 
Applications of Calderon-enhanced integral equation solvers 
range from antenna analysis to the characterization of microwave 
devices and circuits, the analysis of electromagnetic compatibility 
phenomena, and the synthesis of metamaterials. The course will 
cover theoretical and practical issues related to the development 
and implementation of Calderon-enhanced integral equation 
solvers. In addition, the course will detail the incorporation of 
Calderon preconditioners into existing integral equation codes 
and their interaction with fast matrix-vector multiplication schemes. 
Finally, the course will compare Calderon preconditioners 
on theoretical, practical, and performance grounds to other 
preconditioners used in CEM.
SC14	 Internal	Handheld	Device	Antennas:	
Traditional	Design,	Recent	Advances,	and	
Future	Perspectives	for	Bio-Compatible	
Handheld	Device	Antennas
Speaker: Kin-Lu Wong, National Sun Yat-sen University, 
Taiwan
Location: SCC-202C
Internal WWAN and LTE antennas for handheld devices including 
handsets and tablet PCs have recently shown great advances. 
Traditional design was mainly based on λ/4-PIFA. Various planar 
antennas including printed λ/8-monopole, λ/8-PIFA, λ/4-loop 
and λ/4-slot have been demonstrated for achieving much smaller 
size yet wideband operation. These advances will be presented. 
Internal antennas with high radiation efficiency yet low near-
field emission to achieve acceptable HAC and Head/Hand or 
Body SAR values have also been demanded. Such antennas with 
acceptable HAC or SAR values can be treated as bio-compatible 
handheld device antennas, whose design techniques and future 
perspectives will be discussed.

on-siTe social evenTs
Opening Reception (Free)
When: Sunday, July 3, 18:00
Where: Davenport Hotel, Second Floor
The conference will open at 6:00 pm, Sunday, July 3rd, 
with a reception at the gracious Davenport Hotel. Wander 
through the beautiful Hall of Doges, Elizabethan Room, Grand 
Pennington Room, and Marie Antoinette Room and stroll the 
balcony overlooking the Lobby of this elegant property. Hors 
d’oeuvres will be served and no-host bars will be available in 
these spacious reception rooms where conference members 
and guests can visit with friends and colleagues.
Salmon Bake and Fireworks (Free)
When: Monday, July 4, 19:00
Where: Spokane Convention Center, Arbor
A Fourth of July Salmon Bake will be offered at the Convention 
Center on the bank of the Spokane River at 6:30 pm. Since 
this is a national holiday for the United States, we also have 
the opportunity to witness a fireworks display, compliments of 
the City of Spokane. On the other side of the river in Riverfront 
Park will be scores of vendors selling wares and foods for 
the celebration; free concerts from all music genres will be 
performed throughout the day. All conference delegates and 
their companions are invited to enjoy this free dinner and 
entertainment along the riverbank.
Student/GOLD Reception and Lunch (Free)
When: Tuesday, July 5, 12:00 - 13:00
Where: Marie Antoinette Room, Davenport Hotel
The Student/GOLD Reception and lunch is a free event open to 
all student registrants and their advisors as well as Graduates 
of the Last Decade (GOLD).
Women in Engineering Reception (Free)
When: Tuesday, July 5, 17:30 - 19:30
Where: Isabella Room, Davenport Hotel
The IEEE Women in Engineering (WIE) Reception is proudly 
sponsored by the Boeing Company and is open to all 
conference participants. Hors d’oeuvres will be served. The 
scopes of interest of the WIE include increasing the participation 
of women within IEEE, gathering and disseminating information 
regarding the status of women, and initiatives for, by and on 
behalf of women in engineering and science.

 Figure 1. Bolck diagram of designed system configuration. 
Direction-of-Arrival Estimator Using Array 
Switching on Software Defined Radio Platform 
 
Meng-Chang Hua, Cheng-Han Hsu, Wen-Jiao Liao, Chia-Chi Yao, Ting-Hung Yeh and Hsin-Chin Liu 
Department of Electrical Engineering 
National Taiwan University of Science and Technology 
Taipei 106, Taiwan 
hcliu@mail.ntust.edu.tw 
 
 
Abstract—In this work, a 360 degrees direction-of-arrival (DOA) 
estimator using array switching technique is implemented on a 
software defined radio (SDR) platform. The estimator includes a 
square antenna array comprising 16 dipole antennas, which is 
segmented as four 4-element uniform linear arrays (ULA). All 16 
antenna elements are connected to RF switches and then 
connected to four RF receivers. By configuring the switch status 
via software defined radio, one of the ULA is activated for DOA 
estimation using multiple signal classification algorithm. The 
well-known inaccurate DOA estimation near the end-fire of a 
ULA is avoided in this design. Each ULA only estimate signal 
source within its broadside 45  degree azimuth. By switching 
the four ULA, 360-degree azimuth is covered. Because the four 
receivers are phase incoherent, this design includes a phase 
calibration function. Outdoor measurements show that the 
implemented system can estimate the DOA of impinging signals 
with high accuracy even with some multipath reflections. The 
system is very flexible and can easily reconfigure the shape or 
element-number of antenna array by modifying the 
corresponding code on SDR platform.  
Keywords-DOA;software defined radio;array antenna 
I. INTRODUCTION 
Direction-of-arrival (DOA) estimation of multiple signals is 
an important topic in many radar, sonar, radio astronomy and 
mobile communication applications. Many DOA estimation 
algorithms such as multiple signal classification (MUSIC) [1], 
estimation of signal parameter via rotation invariance 
techniques (ESPRIT) [2, 3], and maximum likelihood 
estimator [4], have been studied. Other approaches, such as the 
virtual expansion of array’s aperture size for DOA estimation 
resolution enhancement [5, 6] are also proposed. However, 
these methods cannot accurately estimate DOA information 
when signal sources are located at the end-fire of a uniform 
linear array (ULA). 
Many beam switching antennas designs have been proposed. 
Some comes with simple antenna configurations and control 
circuits [7-9]. In [10], they propose an array antenna 
configuration that is capable of generating 49 beams from 36 
elements to cover the entire hemisphere region. The control 
circuit is made of delay lines and PIN diodes. This technique 
is used in [11] to determine the positions of array elements in 
creating a beam array switching that covers a sector area. In 
[12, 13], a genetic algorithm is used to find appropriate 
combinations of active and parasitic elements to produce 
beams toward desired directions. However the beam coverage, 
gain or switching resolution is often limited. 
In this work, we design a 360-degree azimuth DOA 
estimator using array switching on software defined radio 
(SDR) platform. The estimator includes a square antenna array 
comprising 16 dipole antennas, which is segmented as four 4-
element ULA. Taking the advantages of array switch, the 
inaccurate DOA estimation near the end-fire of a ULA is 
avoided. Outdoor experimental results show that the estimator 
can successfully estimate DOA of impinging signals from 
entire azimuth plane. 
The remainder of the paper is organized as follows. Section 
2 describes the system design. Section 3 shows outdoor 
measurements. Section 4 draws conclusions.  
II. THE PROPOSED SYSTEM DESIGN 
The system design block diagram is illustrated in Fig. 1. An 
array comprising 16 antenna elements is connected to 
switching box 1. Because the system only has four RF 
receivers, only four antenna elements can be connected to RF 
front-ends at once. In order to perform DOA estimation 
algorithms, the phase of all RF receivers need to be 
synchronized. A deterministic source is fed into the channels 
from switching box 2 for receiver phase calibration. Each RF 
receiver down converts RF input signal to intermediate 
frequency (IF) analog signal. A subsequent high speed analog

D. System Operating Flow Chart 
The system operating flow chart is illustrated in Fig. 5. 
First, the signal processing module sends the control signal via 
GPIO ports to the switching box 2. The deterministic signal is 
selected to be received signal; signal processing unit then 
estimates and compensates the phase of all channels. Second, 
the switching box 2 switches to receive the signal from 
antennas, the switching box 1 connects one of four ULA to the 
RF front-end and then perform MUSIC algorithm for DOA 
estimation in signal processing unit. Afterward, the system 
reconfigures the state of switching box 1 and perform DOA 
estimation in the same manner until all zone are scanned. 
Finally, the system combines all estimated results and 
determines the scanning results. In order to maintain system 
reliability, the calibration procedure is executed again before 
starting next DOA estimation.

microwave anechoic chamber beforehand, and then  
國科會補助計畫衍生研發成果推廣資料表
日期:2011/10/21
國科會補助計畫
計畫名稱: 密集讀取器環境被動式超高頻射頻辨識系統之自動佈建研究
計畫主持人: 劉馨勤
計畫編號: 99-2221-E-011-052- 學門領域: 通訊 
研發成果名稱
(中文) 軟體無線電平台之ＲＦＩＤ讀取器設計
(英文) RFID reader design over software defined radio platform
成果歸屬機構
國立臺灣科技大學 發明人
(創作人)
劉馨勤
技術說明
(中文) 目前ＲＦＩＤ讀取器之關鍵技術多由國外大廠掌握，國內ＲＦＩＤ研究大多以採
購國外廠商讀取器晶片或成品讀取機進行，故受限於廠商成品限制，難以進行底
層調變或通訊協定研究。本技術以軟體無線電平台開發ＲＦＩＤ讀取器，其調變
或通訊協定皆可自行設定。藉此技術研究單位可進行ＲＦＩＤ新型標籤或系統研
究。此技術可降低ＲＦＩＤ研發產業之技術門檻，藉此技術研發之產品不受限於
現有標準或規範（現有讀取器晶片或成品多依循現有標準設計），故較有可能申
請相關專利。
(英文) Most key techniques of RFID readers are held by foreign manufactures. Domestic RFID 
research usually uses reader chips or commercial reader products from these 
manufactures. Due to the limitations of these chips or readers, it is difficult to study 
physical layer techniques such as modulations or communication protocols. This 
technique is about how to develop an RFID reader over software defined radio platform, 
which can flexibly define modulation schemes or communication protocols. Domestic 
researchers can study new RFID tags or systems using this technique. This technique 
lowers the technical threshold for RFID research and development industry. The RFID 
industry can use this technique to study new RFID products which are incompatible with 
current standards. It would be easier to obtain some patents for these new products.
產業別 研究發展服務業
技術/產品應用範圍 ＲＦＩＤ研發、應用產業
技術移轉可行性及
預期效益
此技術可降低ＲＦＩＤ研發產業之技術門檻；利用此技術較易研發新型ＲＦＩＤ標籤或
系統。
